Custom installation directory\n    90→2. `$XDG_BIN_DIR` - XDG Base Directory Specification compliant path\n    91→3. `$HOME/bin` - Standard user binary directory (if it exists or can be created)\n    92→4. `$HOME/.opencode/bin` - Default fallback\n    93→\n    94→```bash\n    95→# Examples\n    96→OPENCODE_INSTALL_DIR=/usr/local/bin curl -fsSL https://opencode.ai/install | bash\n    97→XDG_BIN_DIR=$HOME/.local/bin curl -fsSL https://opencode.ai/install | bash\n    98→```\n    99→\n   100→### Agents\n   101→\n   102→OpenCode includes two built-in agents you can switch between with the `Tab` key.\n   103→\n   104→- **build** - Default, full-access agent for development work\n   105→- **plan** - Read-only agent for analysis and code exploration\n   106→  - Denies file edits by default\n   107→  - Asks permission before running bash commands\n   108→  - Ideal for exploring unfamiliar codebases or planning changes\n   109→\n   110→Also included is a **general** subagent for complex searches and multistep tasks.\n   111→This is used internally and can be invoked using `@general` in messages.\n   112→\n   113→Learn more about [agents](https://opencode.ai/docs/agents).\n   114→\n   115→### Documentation\n   116→\n   117→For more info on how to configure OpenCode, [**head over to our docs**](https://opencode.ai/docs).\n   118→\n   119→### Contributing\n   120→\n   121→If you're interested in contributing to OpenCode, please read our [contributing docs](./CONTRIBUTING.md) before submitting a pull request.\n   122→\n   123→### Building on OpenCode\n   124→\n   125→If you are working on a project that's related to OpenCode and is using \"opencode\" as part of its name, for example \"opencode-dashboard\" or \"opencode-mobile\", please add a note to your README to clarify that it is not built by the OpenCode team and is not affiliated with us in any way.\n   126→\n   127→### FAQ\n   128→\n   129→#### How is this different from Claude Code?\n   130→\n   131→It's very similar to Claude Code in terms of capability. Here are the key differences:\n   132→\n   133→- 100% open source\n   134→- Not coupled to any provider. Although we recommend the models we provide through [OpenCode Zen](https://opencode.ai/zen), OpenCode can be used with Claude, OpenAI, Google, or even local models. As models evolve, the gaps between them will close and pricing will drop, so being provider-agnostic is important.\n   135→- Built-in opt-in LSP support\n   136→- A focus on TUI. OpenCode is built by neovim users and the creators of [terminal.shop](https://terminal.shop); we are going to push the limits of what's possible in the terminal.\n   137→- A client/server architecture. This, for example, can allow OpenCode to run on your computer while you drive it remotely from a mobile app, meaning that the TUI frontend is just one of the possible clients.\n   138→\n   139→---\n   140→\n   141→**Join our community** [Discord](https://discord.gg/opencode) | [X.com](https://x.com/opencode)\n   142→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Download directly from the [releases page](https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode/releases) or [opencode.ai/download](https://opencode.ai/download).\n\n| Platform              | Download                           |\n| --------------------- | ---------------------------------- |\n| macOS (Apple Silicon) | `opencode-desktop-mac-arm64.dmg`   |\n| macOS (Intel)         | `opencode-desktop-mac-x64.dmg`     |\n| Windows               | `opencode-desktop-windows-x64.exe` |\n| Linux                 | `.deb`, `.rpm`, or `.AppImage`     |\n\n```bash\n# macOS (Homebrew)\nbrew install --cask opencode-desktop\n# Windows (Scoop)\nscoop bucket add extras; scoop install extras/opencode-desktop\n```\n\n#### Installation Directory\n\nThe install script respects the following priority order for the installation path:\n\n1. `$OPENCODE_INSTALL_DIR` - Custom installation directory\n2. `$XDG_BIN_DIR` - XDG Base Directory Specification compliant path\n3. `$HOME/bin` - Standard user binary directory (if it exists or can be created)\n4. `$HOME/.opencode/bin` - Default fallback\n\n```bash\n# Examples\nOPENCODE_INSTALL_DIR=/usr/local/bin curl -fsSL https://opencode.ai/install | bash\nXDG_BIN_DIR=$HOME/.local/bin curl -fsSL https://opencode.ai/install | bash\n```\n\n### Agents\n\nOpenCode includes two built-in agents you can switch between with the `Tab` key.\n\n- **build** - Default, full-access agent for development work\n- **plan** - Read-only agent for analysis and code exploration\n  - Denies file edits by default\n  - Asks permission before running bash commands\n  - Ideal for exploring unfamiliar codebases or planning changes\n\nAlso included is a **general** subagent for complex searches and multistep tasks.\nThis is used internally and can be invoked using `@general` in messages.\n\nLearn more about [agents](https://opencode.ai/docs/agents).\n\n### Documentation\n\nFor more info on how to configure OpenCode, [**head over to our docs**](https://opencode.ai/docs).\n\n### Contributing\n\nIf you're interested in contributing to OpenCode, please read our [contributing docs](./CONTRIBUTING.md) before submitting a pull request.\n\n### Building on OpenCode\n\nIf you are working on a project that's related to OpenCode and is using \"opencode\" as part of its name, for example \"opencode-dashboard\" or \"opencode-mobile\", please add a note to your README to clarify that it is not built by the OpenCode team and is not affiliated with us in any way.\n\n### FAQ\n\n#### How is this different from Claude Code?\n\nIt's very similar to Claude Code in terms of capability. Here are the key differences:\n\n- 100% open source\n- Not coupled to any provider. Although we recommend the models we provide through [OpenCode Zen](https://opencode.ai/zen), OpenCode can be used with Claude, OpenAI, Google, or even local models. As models evolve, the gaps between them will close and pricing will drop, so being provider-agnostic is important.\n- Built-in opt-in LSP support\n- A focus on TUI. OpenCode is built by neovim users and the creators of [terminal.shop](https://terminal.shop); we are going to push the limits of what's possible in the terminal.\n- A client/server architecture. This, for example, can allow OpenCode to run on your computer while you drive it remotely from a mobile app, meaning that the TUI frontend is just one of the possible clients.\n\n---\n\n**Join our community** [Discord](https://discord.gg/opencode) | [X.com](https://x.com/opencode)\n","numLines":142,"startLine":1,"totalLines":142}}}

{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_06_Gm5gKhauUPPlEExdNAhz6673","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# Contributing to OpenCode\n     2→\n     3→We want to make it easy for you to contribute to OpenCode. Here are the most common type of changes that get merged:\n     4→\n     5→- Bug fixes\n     6→- Additional LSPs / Formatters\n     7→- Improvements to LLM performance\n     8→- Support for new providers\n     9→- Fixes for environment-specific quirks\n    10→- Missing standard behavior\n    11→- Documentation improvements\n    12→\n    13→However, any UI or core product feature must go through a design review with the core team before implementation.\n    14→\n    15→If you are unsure if a PR would be accepted, feel free to ask a maintainer or look for issues with any of the following labels:\n    16→\n    17→- [`help wanted`](https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode/issues?q=is%3Aissue%20state%3Aopen%20label%3Ahelp-wanted)\n    18→- [`good first issue`](https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode/issues?q=is%3Aissue%20state%3Aopen%20label%3A%22good%20first%20issue%22)\n    19→- [`bug`](https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode/issues?q=is%3Aissue%20state%3Aopen%20label%3Abug)\n    20→- [`perf`](https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode/issues?q=is%3Aopen%20is%3Aissue%20label%3A%22perf%22)\n    21→\n    22→> [!NOTE]\n    23→> PRs that ignore these guardrails will likely be closed.\n    24→\n    25→Want to take on an issue? Leave a comment and a maintainer may assign it to you unless it is something we are already working on.\n    26→\n    27→## Adding New Providers\n    28→\n    29→New providers shouldn't require many if ANY code changes, but if you want to add support for a new provider first make a PR to:\n    30→https://github.com/anomalyco/models.dev\n    31→\n    32→## Developing OpenCode\n    33→\n    34→- Requirements: Bun 1.3+\n    35→- Install dependencies and start the dev server from the repo root:\n    36→\n    37→  ```bash\n    38→  bun install\n    39→  bun dev\n    40→  ```\n    41→\n    42→### Running against a different directory\n    43→\n    44→By default, `bun dev` runs OpenCode in the `packages/opencode` directory. To run it against a different directory or repository:\n    45→\n    46→```bash\n    47→bun dev <directory>\n    48→```\n    49→\n    50→To run OpenCode in the root of the opencode repo itself:\n    51→\n    52→```bash\n    53→bun dev .\n    54→```\n    55→\n    56→### Building a \"localcode\"\n    57→\n    58→To compile a standalone executable:\n    59→\n    60→```bash\n    61→./packages/opencode/script/build.ts --single\n    62→```\n    63→\n    64→Then run it with:\n    65→\n    66→```bash\n    67→./packages/opencode/dist/opencode-<platform>/bin/opencode\n    68→```\n    69→\n    70→Replace `<platform>` with your platform (e.g., `darwin-arm64`, `linux-x64`).\n    71→\n    72→- Core pieces:\n    73→  - `packages/opencode`: OpenCode core business logic & server.\n    74→  - `packages/opencode/src/cli/cmd/tui/`: The TUI code, written in SolidJS with [opentui](https://github.com/sst/opentui)\n    75→  - `packages/app`: The shared web UI components, written in SolidJS\n    76→  - `packages/desktop`: The native desktop app, built with Electron (wraps `packages/app`)\n    77→  - `packages/plugin`: Source for `@opencode-ai/plugin`\n    78→\n    79→### Understanding bun dev vs opencode\n    80→\n    81→During development, `bun dev` is the local equivalent of the built `opencode` command. Both run the same CLI interface:\n    82→\n    83→```bash\n    84→# Development (from project root)\n    85→bun dev --help           # Show all available commands\n    86→bun dev serve            # Start headless API server\n    87→bun dev web              # Start server + open web interface\n    88→bun dev <directory>      # Start TUI in specific directory\n    89→\n    90→# Production\n    91→opencode --help          # Show all available commands\n    92→opencode serve           # Start headless API server\n    93→opencode web             # Start server + open web interface\n    94→opencode <directory>     # Start TUI in specific directory\n    95→```\n    96→\n    97→### Running the API Server\n    98→\n    99→To start the OpenCode headless API server:\n   100→\n   101→```bash\n   102→bun dev serve\n   103→```\n   104→\n   105→This starts the headless server on port 4096 by default. You can specify a different port:\n   106→\n   107→```bash\n   108→bun dev serve --port 8080\n   109→```\n   110→\n   111→### Running the Web App\n   112→\n   113→To test UI changes during development:\n   114→\n   115→1. **First, start the OpenCode server** (see [Running the API Server](#running-the-api-server) section above)\n   116→2. **Then run the web app:**\n   117→\n   118→```bash\n   119→bun run --cwd packages/app dev\n   120→```\n   121→\n   122→This starts a local dev server at http://localhost:5173 (or similar port shown in output). Most UI changes can be tested here, but the server must be running for full functionality.\n   123→\n   124→### Running the Desktop App\n   125→\n   126→The desktop app is an Electron application that wraps the web UI.\n   127→\n   128→To run the desktop app in development:\n   129→\n   130→```bash\n   131→bun run --cwd packages/desktop dev\n   132→```\n   133→\n   134→To create a production build and package the app:\n   135→\n   136→```bash\n   137→bun run --cwd packages/desktop build\n   138→bun run --cwd packages/desktop package\n   139→```\n   140→\n   141→> [!NOTE]\n   142→> If you make changes to the API or SDK (e.g. `packages/opencode/src/server/server.ts`), run `./script/generate.ts` to regenerate the SDK and related files.\n   143→\n   144→Please try to follow the [style guide](./AGENTS.md)\n   145→\n   146→### Setting up a Debugger\n   147→\n   148→Bun debugging is currently rough around the edges. We hope this guide helps you get set up and avoid some pain points.\n   149→\n   150→The most reliable way to debug OpenCode is to run it manually in a terminal via `bun run --inspect=<url> dev ...` and attach\n   151→your debugger via that URL. Other methods can result in breakpoints being mapped incorrectly, at least in VSCode (YMMV).\n   152→\n   153→Caveats:\n   154→\n   155→- If you want to run the OpenCode TUI and have breakpoints triggered in the server code, you might need to run `bun dev spawn` instead of\n   156→  the usual `bun dev`. This is because `bun dev` runs the server in a worker thread and breakpoints might not work there.\n   157→- If `spawn` does not work for you, you can debug the server separately:\n   158→  - Debug server: `bun run --inspect=ws://localhost:6499/ --cwd packages/opencode ./src/index.ts serve --port 4096`,\n   159→    then attach TUI with `opencode attach http://localhost:4096`\n   160→  - Debug TUI: `bun run --inspect=ws://localhost:6499/ --cwd packages/opencode --conditions=browser ./src/index.ts`\n   161→\n   162→Other tips and tricks:\n   163→\n   164→- You might want to use `--inspect-wait` or `--inspect-brk` instead of `--inspect`, depending on your workflow\n   165→- Specifying `--inspect=ws://localhost:6499/` on every invocation can be tiresome, you may want to `export BUN_OPTIONS=--inspect=ws://localhost:6499/` instead\n   166→\n   167→#### VSCode Setup\n   168→\n   169→If you use VSCode, you can use our example configurations [.vscode/settings.example.json](.vscode/settings.example.json) and [.vscode/launch.example.json](.vscode/launch.example.json).\n   170→\n   171→Some debug methods that can be problematic:\n   172→\n   173→- Debug configurations with `\"request\": \"launch\"` can have breakpoints incorrectly mapped and thus unusable\n   174→- The same problem arises when running OpenCode in the VSCode `JavaScript Debug Terminal`\n   175→\n   176→With that said, you may want to try these methods, as they might work for you.\n   177→\n   178→## Pull Request Expectations\n   179→\n   180→### Issue First Policy\n   181→\n   182→**All PRs must reference an existing issue.** Before opening a PR, open an issue describing the bug or feature. This helps maintainers triage and prevents duplicate work. PRs without a linked issue may be closed without review.\n   183→\n   184→- Use `Fixes #123` or `Closes #123` in your PR description to link the issue\n   185→- For small fixes, a brief issue is fine - just enough context for maintainers to understand the problem\n   186→\n   187→### General Requirements\n   188→\n   189→- Keep pull requests small and focused\n   190→- Explain the issue and why your change fixes it\n   191→- Before adding new functionality, ensure it doesn't already exist elsewhere in the codebase\n   192→\n   193→### UI Changes\n   194→\n   195→If your PR includes UI changes, please include screenshots or videos showing the before and after. This helps maintainers review faster and gives you quicker feedback.\n   196→\n   197→### Logic Changes\n   198→\n   199→For non-UI changes (bug fixes, new features, refactors), explain **how you verified it works**:\n   200→\n   201→- What did you test?\n   202→- How can a reviewer reproduce/confirm the fix?\n   203→\n   204→### No AI-Generated Walls of Text\n   205→\n   206→Long, AI-generated PR descriptions and issues are not acceptable and may be ignored. Respect the maintainers' time:\n   207→\n   208→- Write short, focused descriptions\n   209→- Explain what changed and why in your own words\n   210→- If you can't explain it briefly, your PR might be too large\n   211→\n   212→### PR Titles\n   213→\n   214→PR titles should follow conventional commit standards:\n   215→\n   216→- `feat:` new feature or functionality\n   217→- `fix:` bug fix\n   218→- `docs:` documentation or README changes\n   219→- `chore:` maintenance tasks, dependency updates, etc.\n   220→- `refactor:` code refactoring without changing behavior\n   221→- `test:` adding or updating tests\n   222→\n   223→You can optionally include a scope to indicate which package is affected:\n   224→\n   225→- `feat(app):` feature in the app package\n   226→- `fix(desktop):` bug fix in the desktop package\n   227→- `chore(opencode):` maintenance in the opencode package\n   228→\n   229→Examples:\n   230→\n   231→- `docs: update contributing guidelines`\n   232→- `fix: resolve crash on startup`\n   233→- `feat: add dark mode support`\n   234→- `feat(app): add dark mode support`\n   235→- `fix(desktop): resolve crash on startup`\n   236→- `chore: bump dependency versions`\n   237→\n   238→### Style Preferences\n   239→\n   240→These are not strictly enforced, they are just general guidelines:\n   241→\n   242→- **Functions:** Keep logic within a single function unless breaking it out adds clear reuse or composition benefits.\n   243→- **Destructuring:** Do not do unnecessary destructuring of variables.\n   244→- **Control flow:** Avoid `else` statements.\n   245→- **Error handling:** Prefer `.catch(...)` instead of `try`/`catch` when possible.\n   246→- **Types:** Reach for precise types and avoid `any`.\n   247→- **Variables:** Stick to immutable patterns and avoid `let`.\n   248→- **Naming:** Choose concise single-word identifiers when they remain descriptive.\n   249→- **Runtime APIs:** Use Bun helpers such as `Bun.file()` when they fit the use case.\n   250→\n   251→## Feature Requests\n   252→\n   253→For net-new functionality, start with a design conversation. Open an issue describing the problem, your proposed approach (optional), and why it belongs in OpenCode. The core team will help decide whether it should move forward; please wait for that approval instead of opening a feature PR directly.\n   254→\n   255→## Trust & Vouch System\n   256→\n   257→This project uses [vouch](https://github.com/mitchellh/vouch) to manage contributor trust. The vouch list is maintained in [`.github/VOUCHED.td`](.github/VOUCHED.td).\n   258→\n   259→### How it works\n   260→\n   261→- **Vouched users** are explicitly trusted contributors.\n   262→- **Denounced users** are explicitly blocked. Issues and pull requests from denounced users are automatically closed. It is not used for disagreements or honest mistakes.\n   281→\n   282→## Issue Requirements\n   283→\n   284→All issues **must** use one of our issue templates:\n   285→\n   286→- **Bug report** — for reporting bugs (requires a description)\n   287→- **Feature request** — for suggesting enhancements (requires verification checkbox and description)\n   288→- **Question** — for asking questions (requires the question)\n   289→\n   290→Blank issues are not allowed. When a new issue is opened, an automated check verifies that it follows a template and meets our contributing guidelines. If an issue doesn't meet the requirements, you'll receive a comment explaining what needs to be fixed and have **2 hours** to edit the issue. After that, it will be automatically closed.\n   291→\n   292→Issues may be flagged for:\n   293→\n   294→- Not using a template\n   295→- Required fields left empty or filled with placeholder text\n   296→- AI-generated walls of text\n   297→- Missing meaningful content\n   298→\n   299→If you believe your issue was incorrectly flagged, let a maintainer know.\n   300→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Leave a comment and a maintainer may assign it to you unless it is something we are already working on.\n\n## Adding New Providers\n\nNew providers shouldn't require many if ANY code changes, but if you want to add support for a new provider first make a PR to:\nhttps://github.com/anomalyco/models.dev\n\n## Developing OpenCode\n\n- Requirements: Bun 1.3+\n- Install dependencies and start the dev server from the repo root:\n\n  ```bash\n  bun install\n  bun dev\n  ```\n\n### Running against a different directory\n\nBy default, `bun dev` runs OpenCode in the `packages/opencode` directory. We hope this guide helps you get set up and avoid some pain points.\n\nThe most reliable way to debug OpenCode is to run it manually in a terminal via `bun run --inspect=<url> dev ...` and attach\nyour debugger via that URL. Other methods can result in breakpoints being mapped incorrectly, at least in VSCode (YMMV).\n\nCaveats:\n\n- If you want to run the OpenCode TUI and have breakpoints triggered in the server code, you might need to run `bun dev spawn` instead of\n  the usual `bun dev`. This helps maintainers triage and prevents duplicate work. PRs without a linked issue may be closed without review.\n\n- Use `Fixes #123` or `Closes #123` in your PR description to link the issue\n- For small fixes, a brief issue is fine - just enough context for maintainers to understand the problem\n\n### General Requirements\n\n- Keep pull requests small and focused\n- Explain the issue and why your change fixes it\n- Before adding new functionality, ensure it doesn't already exist elsewhere in the codebase\n\n### UI Changes\n\nIf your PR includes UI changes, please include screenshots or videos showing the before and after. This helps maintainers review faster and gives you quicker feedback.\n\n### Logic Changes\n\nFor non-UI changes (bug fixes, new features, refactors), explain **how you verified it works**:\n\n- What did you test?\n- How can a reviewer reproduce/confirm the fix?\n\n### No AI-Generated Walls of Text\n\nLong, AI-generated PR descriptions and issues are not acceptable and may be ignored. Respect the maintainers' time:\n\n- Write short, focused descriptions\n- Explain what changed and why in your own words\n- If you can't explain it briefly, your PR might be too large\n\n### PR Titles\n\nPR titles should follow conventional commit standards:\n\n- `feat:` new feature or functionality\n- `fix:` bug fix\n- `docs:` documentation or README changes\n- `chore:` maintenance tasks, dependency updates, etc.\n- `refactor:` code refactoring without changing behavior\n- `test:` adding or updating tests\n\nYou can optionally include a scope to indicate which package is affected:\n\n- `feat(app):` feature in the app package\n- `fix(desktop):` bug fix in the desktop package\n- `chore(opencode):` maintenance in the opencode package\n\nExamples:\n\n- `docs: update contributing guidelines`\n- `fix: resolve crash on startup`\n- `feat: add dark mode support`\n- `feat(app): add dark mode support`\n- `fix(desktop): resolve crash on startup`\n- `chore: bump dependency versions`\n\n### Style Preferences\n\nThese are not strictly enforced, they are just general guidelines:\n\n- **Functions:** Keep logic within a single function unless breaking it out adds clear reuse or composition benefits.\n- **Destructuring:** Do not do unnecessary destructuring of variables.\n- **Control flow:** Avoid `else` statements.\n- **Error handling:** Prefer `.catch(...)` instead of `try`/`catch` when possible.\n- **Types:** Reach for precise types and avoid `any`.\n- **Variables:** Stick to immutable patterns and avoid `let`.\n- **Naming:** Choose concise single-word identifiers when they remain descriptive.\n- **Runtime APIs:** Use Bun helpers such as `Bun.file()` when they fit the use case.\n\n## Feature Requests\n\nFor net-new functionality, start with a design conversation. 文件系统工具 (filesystem.ts)\n- 全局路径/配置 (global.ts)\n- 日志系统 (util/log)\n- 插件系统 (plugin/)\n- 进程管理 (process.ts)\n- NPM 集成 (npm.ts, npm-config.ts)\n\n#### 3. LLM 提供器官 `packages/llm` (@opencode-ai/llm)\n\n独立封装的 LLM 提供商实现：\n- 协议层：Anthropic Messages, OpenAI Chat/Responses, Bedrock Converse, Gemini\n- 提供商实现：Amazon Bedrock, Anthropic, Azure, Cloudflare, GitHub Copilot, Google, OpenAI, OpenRouter, xAI, OpenAI-compatible 等\n\n#### 4. Web UI `packages/app` (@opencode-ai/app)\n\n基于 SolidJS + Vite 的 Web 界面：\n- 通过 WebSocket 连接到 OpenCode 服务器\n- 共享 TUI 和 Web 的 UI 组件\n- i18n 支持（20+ 语言）\n- 通过 `@opencode-ai/ui` 共享组件\n\n#### 5. UI 组件库 `packages/ui` (@opencode-ai/ui)\n\n共享 UI 组件系统：\n- Markdown 渲染（marked + shiki + kaTeX）\n- Diff 展示\n- 文件图标 / 提供商图标\n- Tailwind 样式\n- 动画 (motion)\n\n#### 6. 桌面应用 `packages/desktop` (@opencode-ai/desktop)\n\nElectron 桌面应用：\n- 自动更新 (electron-updater)\n- 原生终端集成 (@lydell/node-pty)\n- 支持 macOS, Windows, Linux\n\n#### 7. 文档网站 `packages/web` (@opencode-ai/web)\n\n基于 Astro + Starlight 的文档和官网，部署到 Cloudflare Pages。\n\n#### 8. 插件系统 `packages/plugin` (@opencode-ai/plugin)\n\n允许第三方开发者扩展 OpenCode，提供：\n- 工具注册 (tool)\n- TUI 扩展 (tui)\n- SDK 集成\n\n---\n\n### 五、架构特点\n\n#### 1. 客户端/服务器架构 (C/S)\nOpenCode 采用客户端-服务器分离架构：\n- **Server**：基于 Effect + Hono + OpenAPI 构建，提供 HTTP API 和 WebSocket\n- **Client**：可以有多种前端——TUI（终端）、Web UI（浏览器）、Desktop App（Electron）\n- 服务器可以通过 mDNS 进行局域网发现\n\n#### 2. 双智能体模式 (Dual Agent)\n- **build** 模式：默认模式，拥有完全的文件访问权限，用于开发工作\n- **plan** 模式：只读模式，用于代码分析和探索\n- **general** 子代理：用于复杂搜索和多步骤任务\n\n#### 3. Effect 函数式编程\n项目广泛使用 Effect 库进行：\n- 依赖注入（Layer/Context 系统）\n- 副作用管理（结构化并发）\n- 错误处理（Schema-based 错误类型）\n- 流式处理（Stream）\n\n#### 4. 多运行时兼容\n通过 `#imports` (subpath imports) 支持 Bun 和 Node.js 双运行时：\n```json\n\"#db\": {\n  \"bun\": \"./src/storage/db.bun.ts\",\n  \"node\": \"./src/storage/db.node.ts\"\n},\n\"#pty\": {\n  \"bun\": \"./src/pty/pty.bun.ts\",\n  \"node\": \"./src/pty/pty.node.ts\"\n}\n```\n\n#### 5. AI 提供商无关设计\n- 通过 Vercel AI SDK 统一接口\n- 20+ AI 提供商支持\n- 可扩展的提供商注册系统\n- 模型目录管理（`models-snapshot.js` 文件大小达 2.5MB）\n\n#### 6. 完整的工具系统\nAI Agent 可以使用 20+ 工具：\n- 文件操作：read, write, edit, apply_patch, glob, grep\n- 命令执行：shell, plan\n- 网络：webfetch, websearch\n- 项目管理：repo_overview, repo_clone\n- LSP 支持：lsp\n- MCP (Model Context Protocol) 支持\n- 自定义技能（skill）\n\n#### 7. 云基础设施\n- SST 用于基础设施即代码\n- 部署到 Cloudflare Workers/Pages\n- 包含企业版部署配置\n- 使用 Stripe 处理支付\n- Honeycomb 监控和 OpenTelemetry 追踪\n\n#### 8. 丰富的 CI/CD\n- 28 个 GitHub Actions 工作流\n- 自动化发布流程（macOS, Windows, Linux）\n- 自动生成 SDK\n- 多语言文档同步\n- Issue/PR 自动管理\n\n---\n\n### 六、依赖关系\n\n#### 主要运行时依赖 (Root + workspace 聚合)\n\n**AI 和机器学习：**\n- `ai`, `@ai-sdk/*` (15+ 个 SDK 包) - Vercel AI SDK 生态\n- `@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider`, `ai-gateway-provider` - 第三方 AI 网关\n- `gitlab-ai-provider`, `venice-ai-sdk-provider` - 特殊提供商\n\n**框架和核心：**\n- `solid-js`, `@solidjs/*` (router, meta, start) - UI 框架\n- `effect`, `@effect/*` (platform-node, opentelemetry) - 函数式编程\n- `hono`, `hono-openapi` - HTTP 框架\n- `zod` - 数据验证\n- `yargs` - CLI 参数解析\n\n**UI 和渲染：**\n- `@opentui/*` (core, solid, keymap) - 终端 UI 框架\n- `@kobalte/core` - 无障碍组件\n- `tailwindcss` - CSS 框架\n- `marked`, `shiki` - Markdown 渲染和语法高亮\n- `motion` - 动画库\n- `vitrua`, `solid-list` - 虚拟列表\n\n**数据库：**\n- `drizzle-orm`, `drizzle-kit` - ORM\n- `@aws-sdk/client-s3` - S3 存储\n\n**桌面端特有：**\n- `electron`, `@tsconfig/bun` - TS 配置\n- `sst` - 云部署\n- `@playwright/test` - E2E 测试\n\n#### 工作空间包依赖图\n\n```\nopencode (根)\n├── @opencode-ai/core          # 核心共享库\n│   └── effect, ai-sdk, cross-spawn, immer, (@opencode-ai/core)\n\n包含跨包共享的基础设施：\n- 认证 (auth.ts)\n- AI 提供商和模型目录 (provider.ts, models.ts, catalog.ts)\n- 文件系统工具 (filesystem.ts)\n- 全局路径/配置 (global.ts)\n- 日志系统 (util/log)\n- 插件系统 (plugin/)\n- 进程管理 (process.ts)\n- NPM 集成 (npm.ts, npm-config.ts)\n\n#### 3. LLM 提供器官 `packages/llm` (@opencode-ai/llm)\n\n独立封装的 LLM 提供商实现：\n- 协议层：Anthropic Messages, OpenAI Chat/Responses, Bedrock Converse, Gemini\n- 提供商实现：Amazon Bedrock, Anthropic, Azure, Cloudflare, GitHub Copilot, Google, OpenAI, OpenRouter, xAI, OpenAI-compatible 等\n\n#### 4. Web UI `packages/app` (@opencode-ai/app)\n\n基于 SolidJS + Vite 的 Web 界面：\n- 通过 WebSocket 连接到 OpenCode 服务器\n- 共享 TUI 和 Web 的 UI 组件\n- i18n 支持（20+ 语言）\n- 通过 `@opencode-ai/ui` 共享组件\n\n#### 5. UI 组件库 `packages/ui` (@opencode-ai/ui)\n\n共享 UI 组件系统：\n- Markdown 渲染（marked + shiki + kaTeX）\n- Diff 展示\n- 文件图标 / 提供商图标\n- Tailwind 样式\n- 动画 (motion)\n\n#### 6. 桌面应用 `packages/desktop` (@opencode-ai/desktop)\n\nElectron 桌面应用：\n- 自动更新 (electron-updater)\n- 原生终端集成 (@lydell/node-pty)\n- 支持 macOS, Windows, Linux\n\n#### 7. 文档网站 `packages/web` (@opencode-ai/web)\n\n基于 Astro + Starlight 的文档和官网，部署到 Cloudflare Pages。\n\n#### 8. 插件系统 `packages/plugin` (@opencode-ai/plugin)\n\n允许第三方开发者扩展 OpenCode，提供：\n- 工具注册 (tool)\n- TUI 扩展 (tui)\n- SDK 集成\n\n---\n\n### 五、架构特点\n\n#### 1. 客户端/服务器架构 (C/S)\nOpenCode 采用客户端-服务器分离架构：\n- **Server**：基于 Effect + Hono + OpenAPI 构建，提供 HTTP API 和 WebSocket\n- **Client**：可以有多种前端——TUI（终端）、Web UI（浏览器）、Desktop App（Electron）\n- 服务器可以通过 mDNS 进行局域网发现\n\n#### 2. 双智能体模式 (Dual Agent)\n- **build** 模式：默认模式，拥有完全的文件访问权限，用于开发工作\n- **plan** 模式：只读模式，用于代码分析和探索\n- **general** 子代理：用于复杂搜索和多步骤任务\n\n#### 3. Effect 函数式编程\n项目广泛使用 Effect 库进行：\n- 依赖注入（Layer/Context 系统）\n- 副作用管理（结构化并发）\n- 错误处理（Schema-based 错误类型）\n- 流式处理（Stream）\n\n#### 4. 多运行时兼容\n通过 `#imports` (subpath imports) 支持 Bun 和 Node.js 双运行时：\n```json\n\"#db\": {\n  \"bun\": \"./src/storage/db.bun.ts\",\n  \"node\": \"./src/storage/db.node.ts\"\n},\n\"#pty\": {\n  \"bun\": \"./src/pty/pty.bun.ts\",\n  \"node\": \"./src/pty/pty.node.ts\"\n}\n```\n\n#### 5. AI 提供商无关设计\n- 通过 Vercel AI SDK 统一接口\n- 20+ AI 提供商支持\n- 可扩展的提供商注册系统\n- 模型目录管理（`models-snapshot.js` 文件大小达 2.5MB）\n\n#### 6. 完整的工具系统\nAI Agent 可以使用 20+ 工具：\n- 文件操作：read, write, edit, apply_patch, glob, grep\n- 命令执行：shell, plan\n- 网络：webfetch, websearch\n- 项目管理：repo_overview, repo_clone\n- LSP 支持：lsp\n- MCP (Model Context Protocol) 支持\n- 自定义技能（skill）\n\n#### 7. 云基础设施\n- SST 用于基础设施即代码\n- 部署到 Cloudflare Workers/Pages\n- 包含企业版部署配置\n- 使用 Stripe 处理支付\n- Honeycomb 监控和 OpenTelemetry 追踪\n\n#### 8. 丰富的 CI/CD\n- 28 个 GitHub Actions 工作流\n- 自动化发布流程（macOS, Windows, Linux）\n- 自动生成 SDK\n- 多语言文档同步\n- Issue/PR 自动管理\n\n---\n\n### 六、依赖关系\n\n#### 主要运行时依赖 (Root + workspace 聚合)\n\n**AI 和机器学习：**\n- `ai`, `@ai-sdk/*` (15+ 个 SDK 包) - Vercel AI SDK 生态\n- `@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider`, `ai-gateway-provider` - 第三方 AI 网关\n- `gitlab-ai-provider`, `venice-ai-sdk-provider` - 特殊提供商\n\n**框架和核心：**\n- `solid-js`, `@solidjs/*` (router, meta, start) - UI 框架\n- `effect`, `@effect/*` (platform-node, opentelemetry) - 函数式编程\n- `hono`, `hono-openapi` - HTTP 框架\n- `zod` - 数据验证\n- `yargs` - CLI 参数解析\n\n**UI 和渲染：**\n- `@opentui/*` (core, solid, keymap) - 终端 UI 框架\n- `@kobalte/core` - 无障碍组件\n- `tailwindcss` - CSS 框架\n- `marked`, `shiki` - Markdown 渲染和语法高亮\n- `motion` - 动画库\n- `vitrua`, `solid-list` - 虚拟列表\n\n**数据库：**\n- `drizzle-orm`, `drizzle-kit` - ORM\n- `@aws-sdk/client-s3` - S3 存储\n\n**桌面端特有：**\n- `electron`, `electron-builder`, `electron-vite`\n- `@lydell/node-pty` - 伪终端\n- `electron-updater`, `electron-store`, `electron-log`\n\n**开发依赖：**\n- `turbo` - Monorepo 构建\n- `oxlint` - 静态分析\n- `typescript`, `@tsconfig/bun` - TS 配置\n- `sst` - 云部署\n- `@playwright/test` - E2E 测试\n\n#### 工作空间包依赖图\n\n```\nopencode (根)\n├── @opencode-ai/core          # 核心共享库\n│   └── effect, ai-sdk, cross-spawn, immer, zod...\n├── opencode                   # 主包（全部业务逻辑）\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/core      # 依赖 core\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/plugin    # 依赖 plugin\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/script    # 依赖 script  \n│   ├── @opencode-ai/sdk       # 依赖 sdk\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/ui        # 依赖 ui\n│   └── 大量第三方依赖...\n├── @opencode-ai/app           # Web UI\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/ui        # 依赖 UI\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/sdk       # 依赖 SDK\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/core      # 依赖 core\n│   ├── @kobalte/core\n│   └── solid-js, tailwindcss...\n├── @opencode-ai/ui            # 共享 UI 组件\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/core      # 依赖 core\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/sdk       # 依赖 SDK\n│   ├── @kobalte/core\n│   └── marked, shiki, motion...\n├── @opencode-ai/desktop       # Electron 桌面应用\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/app       # 依赖 app\n│   └── @opencode-ai/ui        # 依赖 UI\n├── @opencode-ai/web           # 文档网站 (Astro)\n│   └── opencode (workspace)   # 依赖主包\n├── @opencode-ai/llm           # LLM 提供商\n│   └── effect\n├── @opencode-ai/plugin        # 插件 SDK\n│   ├── @opencode-ai/sdk\n│   ├── effect, zod\n│   └── @opentui/* (可选)\n└── @opencode-ai/sdk (js/)     # 开发者 SDK\n```\n\n---\n\n### 七、总结\n\n**OpenCode** 是一个**开源的 AI 编程代理**（AI Coding Agent），定位为 Claude Code 的开源替代品。其核心区别在于：\n\n1. **100% 开源** - MIT 许可证\n2. **提供商无关** - 支持 20+ AI 模型提供商，不锁定在任何单一服务\n3. **终端优先** - 基于 OpenTUI 构建了强大的终端用户界面\n4. **客户端/服务器架构** - 支持 TUI、Web、Desktop 多种前端，甚至可以远程驱动\n\n项目是一个大型 TypeScript monorepo，由大约 30 个工作空间包组成，代码规模初步估计在 **30万-50万行** 级别（仅 `packages/opencode/src/session/prompt.ts` 就达 88K 行，`models-snapshot.js` 达 2.5MB）。技术选型现代且先进，大量使用函数式编程范式（Effect）和响应式 UI（SolidJS）。"}],"totalDurationMs":84071,"totalTokens":65827,"totalToolUseCount":50,"usage":{"input_tokens":4663,"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":56064,"output_tokens":5100,"service_tier":"standard"}}}
